local v19 = loadstring([=[local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService");
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService");
local TextService = game:GetService("TextService");

local Player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer;

local NotifGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui");
NotifGui.Name = "AkaliNotif";
NotifGui.Parent = RunService:IsStudio() and Player.PlayerGui or game:GetService("CoreGui");

local Container = Instance.new("Frame");
Container.Name = "Container";
Container.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0.5, -20);
Container.Size = UDim2.new(0, 300, 0.5, 0);
Container.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
Container.Parent = NotifGui;

local function Image(ID, Button)
	local NewImage = Instance.new(string.format("Image%s", Button and "Button" or "Label"));
	NewImage.Image = ID;
	NewImage.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
	return NewImage;
end

local function Round2px()
	local NewImage = Image("http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5761488251");
	NewImage.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Slice;
	NewImage.SliceCenter = Rect.new(2, 2, 298, 298);
	NewImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30);
	return NewImage;
end

local function Shadow2px()
	local NewImage = Image("http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=5761498316");
	NewImage.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Slice;
	NewImage.SliceCenter = Rect.new(17, 17, 283, 283);
	NewImage.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 1) + UDim2.fromOffset(30, 30);
	NewImage.Position = -UDim2.fromOffset(15, 15);
	NewImage.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(30, 30, 30);
	return NewImage;
end

local Padding = 10;
local DescriptionPadding = 10;
local InstructionObjects = {};
local TweenTime = 1;
local TweenStyle = Enum.EasingStyle.Sine;
local TweenDirection = Enum.EasingDirection.Out;

local LastTick = tick();

local function CalculateBounds(TableOfObjects)
	local TableOfObjects = typeof(TableOfObjects) == "table" and TableOfObjects or {};
	local X, Y = 0, 0;
	for _, Object in next, TableOfObjects do
		X += Object.AbsoluteSize.X;
		Y += Object.AbsoluteSize.Y;
	end
	return {X = X, Y = Y, x = X, y = Y};
end

local CachedObjects = {};

local function Update()
	local DeltaTime = tick() - LastTick;
	local PreviousObjects = {};
	for CurObj, Object in next, InstructionObjects do
		local Label, Delta, Done = Object[1], Object[2], Object[3];
		if (not Done) then
			if (Delta < TweenTime) then
				Object[2] = math.clamp(Delta + DeltaTime, 0, 1);
				Delta = Object[2];
			else
				Object[3] = true;
			end
		end
		local NewValue = TweenService:GetValue(Delta, TweenStyle, TweenDirection);
		local CurrentPos = Label.Position;
		local PreviousBounds = CalculateBounds(PreviousObjects);
		local TargetPos = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, PreviousBounds.Y + (Padding * #PreviousObjects));
		Label.Position = CurrentPos:Lerp(TargetPos, NewValue);
		table.insert(PreviousObjects, Label);
	end
	CachedObjects = PreviousObjects;
	LastTick = tick();
end

RunService:BindToRenderStep("UpdateList", 0, Update);

local TitleSettings = {
	Font = Enum.Font.GothamSemibold;
	Size = 14;
}

local DescriptionSettings = {
	Font = Enum.Font.Gotham;
	Size = 14;
}

local MaxWidth = (Container.AbsoluteSize.X - Padding - DescriptionPadding);

local function Label(Text, Font, Size, Button)
	local Label = Instance.new(string.format("Text%s", Button and "Button" or "Label"));
	Label.Text = Text;
	Label.Font = Font;
	Label.TextSize = Size;
	Label.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
	Label.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left;
	Label.RichText = true;
	Label.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);
	return Label;
end

local function TitleLabel(Text)
	return Label(Text, TitleSettings.Font, TitleSettings.Size);
end

local function DescriptionLabel(Text)
	return Label(Text, DescriptionSettings.Font, DescriptionSettings.Size);
end

local PropertyTweenOut = {
	Text = "TextTransparency",
	Fram = "BackgroundTransparency",
	Imag = "ImageTransparency"
}

local function FadeProperty(Object)
	local Prop = PropertyTweenOut[string.sub(Object.ClassName, 1, 4)];
	TweenService:Create(Object, TweenInfo.new(0.25, TweenStyle, TweenDirection), {
		[Prop] = 1;
	}):Play();
end

local function SearchTableFor(Table, For)
	for _, v in next, Table do
		if (v == For) then
			return true;
		end
	end
	return false;
end

local function FindIndexByDependency(Table, Dependency)
	for Index, Object in next, Table do
		if (typeof(Object) == "table") then
			local Found = SearchTableFor(Object, Dependency);
			if (Found) then
				return Index;
			end
		else
			if (Object == Dependency) then
				return Index;
			end
		end
	end
end

local function ResetObjects()
	for _, Object in next, InstructionObjects do
		Object[2] = 0;
		Object[3] = false;
	end
end

local function FadeOutAfter(Object, Seconds)
	wait(Seconds);
	FadeProperty(Object);
	for _, SubObj in next, Object:GetDescendants() do
		FadeProperty(SubObj);
	end
	wait(0.25);
	table.remove(InstructionObjects, FindIndexByDependency(InstructionObjects, Object));
	ResetObjects();
end

return {
	Notify = function(Properties)
		local Properties = typeof(Properties) == "table" and Properties or {};
		local Title = Properties.Title;
		local Description = Properties.Description;
		local Duration = Properties.Duration or 5;
		if (Title) or (Description) then -- Check that user has provided title and/or description
			local Y = Title and 26 or 0;
			if (Description) then
				local TextSize = TextService:GetTextSize(Description, DescriptionSettings.Size, DescriptionSettings.Font, Vector2.new(0, 0));
				for i = 1, math.ceil(TextSize.X / MaxWidth) do
					Y += TextSize.Y;
				end
				Y += 8;
			end
			local NewLabel = Round2px();
			NewLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, Y);
			NewLabel.Position = UDim2.new(-1, 20, 0, CalculateBounds(CachedObjects).Y + (Padding * #CachedObjects));
			if (Title) then
				local NewTitle = TitleLabel(Title);
				NewTitle.Size = UDim2.new(1, -10, 0, 26);
				NewTitle.Position = UDim2.fromOffset(10, 0);
				NewTitle.Parent = NewLabel;
			end
			if (Description) then
				local NewDescription = DescriptionLabel(Description);
				NewDescription.TextWrapped = true;
				NewDescription.Size = UDim2.fromScale(1, 1) + UDim2.fromOffset(-DescriptionPadding, Title and -26 or 0);
				NewDescription.Position = UDim2.fromOffset(10, Title and 26 or 0);
				NewDescription.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment[Title and "Top" or "Center"];
				NewDescription.Parent = NewLabel;
			end
			Shadow2px().Parent = NewLabel;
			NewLabel.Parent = Container;
			table.insert(InstructionObjects, {NewLabel, 0, false});
			coroutine.wrap(FadeOutAfter)(NewLabel, Duration);
		end
	end,
}
]=])().Notify

local vu49 = 0
function StopAudio()
	game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("MainEvent"):FireServer("BoomboxStop")
end
function stop(pu50, pu51)
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu49
	coroutine.wrap(function()
							-- upvalues: (ref) pu50, (ref) vu49, (ref) pu51
		wait(OWNER.Character.LowerTorso.BOOMBOXSOUND.TimeLength - 0.1)
		if OWNER.Character.LowerTorso.BOOMBOXSOUND.SoundId == "rbxassetid://" .. pu50 and vu49 == pu51 then
			StopAudio()
		end
	end)()
end
function Play(pu52)
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu49
	if OWNER.Backpack:FindFirstChild("[Boombox]") then
		local v53 = nil
		OWNER.Backpack["[Boombox]"].Parent = OWNER.Character
		game.ReplicatedStorage.MainEvent:FireServer("Boombox", pu52)
		OWNER.Character["[Boombox]"].RequiresHandle = false
		OWNER.Character["[Boombox]"].Parent = OWNER.Backpack
		OWNER.PlayerGui.MainScreenGui.BoomboxFrame.Visible = false
		if v53 ~= true and v53 then
			v53.Parent = OWNER.Character
		end
		OWNER.Character.LowerTorso:WaitForChild("BOOMBOXSOUND")
		coroutine.wrap(function()
								-- upvalues: (ref) pu52, (ref) vu49
			repeat
				wait()
			until OWNER.Character.LowerTorso.BOOMBOXSOUND.SoundId == "rbxassetid://" .. pu52 and OWNER.Character.LowerTorso.BOOMBOXSOUND.TimeLength > 0.01
			vu49 = vu49 + 1
			stop(pu52, vu49)
		end)()
	end
end

		end
	end

function isNumber(p193)
	return tonumber(p193) ~= nil or p193 == "inf"
end
local vu194 = 1
local function v198()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu191, (ref) vu194
	local v195 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character
	local v196
	if v195 then
		v196 = v195:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
	else
		v196 = v195
	end
	if vu191 and (v195 and (v196 and (v196.Parent and v196.MoveDirection.Magnitude > 0))) then
		local v197 = v196.MoveDirection
		if vu194 and isNumber(vu194) then
			v195:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(v195.PrimaryPart.CFrame + v197 * vu194)
		else
			v195:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(v195.PrimaryPart.CFrame + v197)
		end
	end
end
game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(v198)

		vu200 = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			if getgenv().Underground then
				local v202 = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, -getgenv().UndergroundAmount, 0)
				game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = v202
			end
		end)
	else
		getgenv().Underground = false
		if vu200 then
			vu200:Disconnect()
			vu200 = nil
		end
	end
end)

	local vu216 = game.Players.LocalPlayer

	local vu218 = vu216.GetMouse(v217)
	local vu219 = Instance.new("Tool")

	vu219.Name = "Anti Exploiters"

							-- upvalues: (ref) vu216, (ref) vu219
		local v220 = vu216.Backpack

			vu219.Parent = v220
		end
	end
	vu219.Activated:Connect(function()
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu218
		local v222 = vu218.Hit + Vector3.new(0, 2.5, 0)
		CFrame.new(v222.X, v222.Y, v222.Z)
		game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(true, "X", false, game)
	end)
	vu216.CharacterAdded:Connect(v221)
	v221()
	local vu223 = "X"
	getgenv().Finobe1 = true
	local vu224 = CFrame.new
	local vu225 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local v226 = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local vu227 = game:GetService("RunService")
	local vu228 = nil
	vu227.heartbeat:Connect(function()
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu225, (ref) vu224, (ref) vu228, (ref) vu227
		if vu225.Character then
			local v229 = vu225.Character.HumanoidRootPart
			local v230 = v229.CFrame * vu224(9000000000, 0 / 0, math.huge)
			if getgenv().Finobe1 then
				vu228 = v229.CFrame
				v229.CFrame = v230
				vu227.RenderStepped:Wait()
				v229.CFrame = vu228
			end
		end
	end)
	v226.InputBegan:Connect(function(p231)
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu223, (ref) vu225, (ref) vu228
		if p231.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode[vu223] then
			getgenv().Finobe1 = not getgenv().Finobe1
			if Finobe1 then
				vu228 = nil
				game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
					["Title"] = "Destroy Exploiters",
					["Text"] = "Enabled"
				})
			else
				vu225.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = vu228
				game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
					["Title"] = "Destroy Exploiters",
					["Text"] = "Disabled"
				})
			end
		end
	end)
	local vu232 = nil
	vu232 = hookmetamethod(game, "__index", newcclosure(function(p233, p234)
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu225, (ref) vu228, (ref) vu232
		if checkcaller() or (p234 ~= "CFrame" or not (getgenv().Finobe1 and vu225.Character)) or (not vu225.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or (not vu225.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") or (vu225.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health <= 0 or (p233 ~= vu225.Character.HumanoidRootPart or vu228 == nil)))) then
			return vu232(p233, p234)
		else
			return vu228
		end
	end))
end)

			playing:AdjustSpeed(p278)
		else
			playing:AdjustSpeed(1)
		end

			end

	function getClosestPlayerToCursor()
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu603, (ref) vu604
		local v634 = Settings.Kalslock.FOV
		local v635, v636, v637 = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
		local v638 = nil
		while true do
			local v639
			v637, v639 = v635(v636, v637)
			if v637 == nil then
				break
			end
			if v639 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v639.Character and (v639.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and v639.Character.Humanoid.Health ~= 0 and v639.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
				local v640 = vu603:WorldToViewportPoint(v639.Character.PrimaryPart.Position)
				local v641 = (Vector2.new(v640.X, v640.Y) - Vector2.new(vu604.X, vu604.Y)).magnitude
				if v641 < v634 then
					v638 = v639
					v634 = v641
				end
			end
		end
		return v638
	end

local vu1419 = false
function KnifeAttack()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu1419
	if vu1419 then
							-- ::l3::
		if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("[Knife]") then
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("[Knife]"):Activate()
		else
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("[Knife]").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
		end
		return
	else
		local v1420 = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local v1421 = v1420.Character
		while true do
			if v1421 and v1421:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				v1421.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = game.Workspace.Ignored.Shop["[Knife] - $159"].Head.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -5, 0)
				v1421.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
				fireclickdetector(game.Workspace.Ignored.Shop["[Knife] - $159"].ClickDetector)
			end
			task.wait(0.01)
			if v1420.Backpack:FindFirstChild("[Knife]") then
				vu1419 = true
									-- goto l3
			end
		end
	end
end

function FistAttack()
	if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Combat") then
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Combat"):Activate()
	else
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Combat").Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
	end
end
v1412.CreateDropdown("Attack Method", {
	"Combat",
	"Knife",
	"Bat",
	"Pitchfork"
}, function(p1428)
	_G.attackMethod = p1428
end)
local function vu1429()
	if _G.attackMethod ~= "Knife" then
		if _G.attackMethod ~= "Pitchfork" then
			if _G.attackMethod ~= "Bat" then
				FistAttack()
			else
				BatAttack()
			end
		else
			PitchAttack()
		end
	else
		KnifeAttack()
	end
end
v1412:NewButton("Goto", function()
	local v1430 = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
	if _G.targetPlayer and _G.targetPlayer.Character then
		local v1431 = _G.targetPlayer
		local v1432 = v1431.Character.Head.Position
		local v1433 = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
		if v1433 then
			local v1434, v1435, v1436 = pairs(v1433:GetDescendants())
			local v1437 = {
				["FrontWheel"] = true,
				["Forks"] = true,
				["Pedals"] = true,
				["BackWheel"] = true,
				["RightWheel"] = true,
				["RightPedal"] = true,
				["LeftPedal"] = true,
				["Bell"] = true
			}
			while true do
				local v1438
				v1436, v1438 = v1434(v1435, v1436)
				if v1436 == nil then
					break
				end
				if (v1438:IsA("BasePart") or v1438:IsA("UnionOperation")) and (not v1437[v1438.Name] and (v1438.Name == v1430.Name and not v1438.Anchored)) then
					v1438.Position = v1432
				end
			end
		else
			warn("Vehicles folder not found in Workspace.")
		end
		v1430.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = v1431.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	else
		print("Target player does not have a character or is not found.")
	end
end)

function Fling()
	local v1507, v1508, v1509 = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants())
	while true do
		local v1510
		v1509, v1510 = v1507(v1508, v1509)
		if v1509 == nil then
			break
		end
		if v1510:IsA("BasePart") then
			v1510.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(1, 1, 1, 1, 1)
		end
	end
	local v1511 = Instance.new("BodyGyro", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head)
	local v1512 = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head)
	v1511.P = 90000
	v1511.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9000000000, 9000000000, 9000000000)
	v1511.CFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head.CFrame
	v1512.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	v1512.maxForce = Vector3.new(9000000000, 9000000000, 9000000000)
	local v1513 = Instance.new("BodyThrust")
	v1513.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head
	v1513.Force = Vector3.new(900000, 900000, 900000)
	v1513.Location = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position
end
function StopFling()
	local v1514, v1515, v1516 = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants())
	while true do
		local v1517
		v1516, v1517 = v1514(v1515, v1516)
		if v1516 == nil then
			break
		end
		if v1517:IsA("BodyVelocity") or (v1517:IsA("BodyGyro") or (v1517:IsA("RocketPropulsion") or (v1517:IsA("BodyThrust") or (v1517:IsA("BodyAngularVelocity") or (v1517:IsA("AngularVelocity") or (v1517:IsA("BodyForce") or (v1517:IsA("VectorForce") or v1517:IsA("LineForce")))))))) then
			v1517:Destroy()
		end
	end
	local v1518, v1519, v1520 = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetDescendants())
	while true do
		local v1521
		v1520, v1521 = v1518(v1519, v1520)
		if v1520 == nil then
			break
		end
		if v1521:IsA("BasePart") then
			v1521.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
			v1521.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		end
	end
end

v1812:NewTextbox("Player Name", function(pu1813)
	local v1814, v1815, v1816 = ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
	local v1817 = nil
	while true do
		local v1818
		v1816, v1818 = v1814(v1815, v1816)
		if v1816 == nil then
			v1818 = v1817
			break
		end
		if string.find(string.lower(v1818.Name), string.lower(pu1813), 1, true) or string.find(string.lower(v1818.DisplayName), string.lower(pu1813), 1, true) then
			break
		end
	end
	if v1818 then
		_G.targetPlayer = v1818
	else
		local v1819, v1820 = pcall(function()
								-- upvalues: (ref) pu1813
			return game.Players:GetUserIdFromNameAsync(pu1813)
		end)
		if v1819 then
			_G.targetPlayer = {
				["UserId"] = v1820,
				["Name"] = pu1813
			}
		end
	end
end)
local vu1821 = false
local vu1822 = false
v1812:NewToggle("Server Snipe", function(p1823)
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu1822, (ref) vu1821
	if p1823 then
		local vu1824 = game:GetService("Players")
		local vu1825 = game:GetService("TeleportService")
		local vu1826 = game:GetService("HttpService")
		local function vu1829(p1827, p1828)
			game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
				["Title"] = p1827,
				["Text"] = p1828,
				["Duration"] = 3
			})
		end
		local vu1830 = nil
		if syn and syn.request then
			vu1830 = syn.request
		elseif request then
			vu1830 = request
		elseif http and http.request then
			vu1830 = http.request
		elseif http_request then
			vu1830 = http_request
		else
			vu1829("Error", "Your executor does not support http requests")
		end
		local function vu1832(p1831)
								-- upvalues: (ref) vu1830, (ref) vu1826
			return vu1826:JSONDecode(vu1830({
				["Url"] = "https://thumbnails.roblox.com/v1/users/avatar-headshot?userIds=" .. p1831 .. "&size=48x48&format=Png&isCircular=false"
			}).Body).data[1].imageUrl
		end
		local function vu1847(p1833)
								-- upvalues: (ref) vu1826, (ref) vu1830
			local v1834, v1835, v1836 = ipairs(p1833)
			local v1837 = {}
			local v1838 = "https://thumbnails.roblox.com/v1/batch"
			while true do
				local v1839
				v1836, v1839 = v1834(v1835, v1836)
				if v1836 == nil then
					break
				end
				table.insert(v1837, {
					["token"] = v1839,
					["type"] = "AvatarHeadShot",
					["size"] = "48x48",
					["isCircular"] = false
				})
			end
			local v1840 = vu1830({
				["Url"] = v1838,
				["Method"] = "POST",
				["Headers"] = {
					["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
				},
				["Body"] = vu1826:JSONEncode(v1837)
			}).Body
			local v1841 = vu1826
			local v1842, v1843, v1844 = ipairs(v1841:JSONDecode(v1840).data)
			local v1845 = {}
